===== RESPONSE =====
**Incident Report**

Most likely root cause: the sign-in client component intentionally renders different text on the server and client.

Evidence:
- In [LoginComponent.tsx](/home/dmytro/Github/phd-work/nextcrm-app-update/app/[locale]/(auth)/sign-in/components/LoginComponent.tsx:36), the card title is computed as:

```ts
typeof window === "undefined" ? "Login" : "Sign in"
```

- React’s incident diff reports exactly that mismatch:
  - Server HTML: `Login`
  - Client render: `Sign in`

This is deterministic. Next.js still server-renders Client Components for the initial HTML, so `typeof window === "undefined"` is true during SSR and false during browser hydration. React then sees different text in the same node and throws the hydration mismatch.

Secondary matching issue:
- [LoginComponent.tsx](/home/dmytro/Github/phd-work/nextcrm-app-update/app/[locale]/(auth)/sign-in/components/LoginComponent.tsx:37) also branches the divider text:
  - Server: `Or continue with email`
  - Client: `Or continue with Email`

Likely introducing change:
- `git blame` points both divergent branches to commit `9be250f` from 2026-05-01: `Polish sign-in copy and labels`.
- The incident occurred on 2026-05-04, after that commit.

Confidence: high. The observed error text, route, component stack, and exact string diff all match the current source code. No code changes were made.

    31	export function LoginComponent() {
    32	  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
    33	  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>("email");
    34	  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");

    17	type Props = {
    18	  children: ReactNode;
    19	  params: Promise<{ locale: string }>;
    20	};
    21	
    22	export async function generateMetadata(props: Props) {
    23	  const params = await props.params;
    24	
    25	  const { locale } = params;
    26	
    27	  const t = await getTranslations({ locale, namespace: "RootLayout" });
    28

    32	    description: t("description"),

    34	      images: [
    35	        {

    37	          width: 1200,
    38	          height: 630,

    40	        },

    46	      width: 1200,
    47	      height: 630,
    48	      alt: t("title"),
    49	    },
    50	  };
    51	}
    52	
    53	export default async function RootLayout(props: Props) {
    54	  const params = await props.params;
    55	
    56	  const { locale } = params;
    57	
    58	  const { children } = props;
    59	
    60	  const messages = await getMessages();
    61	
    62	  return (
    63	    <html lang={locale} suppressHydrationWarning>
    64	      <body className={inter.className + " min-h-screen"}>
    65	        <NextIntlClientProvider locale={locale} messages={messages}>
    66	          <ThemeProvider attribute="class" defaultTheme="system" enableSystem>

    68	            {children}
    69	          </ThemeProvider>
    70	        </NextIntlClientProvider>

    73	      </body>
    74	    </html>

codex
The working tree has no local diff in that component, and the migration plan still shows the original static `Login`/`Or continue with email` copy. The current branch’s latest commit changed those to client-dependent values, which is sufficient to produce the React hydration error every time that path is server-rendered.

codex
**Incident Report**

Most likely root cause: the sign-in client component intentionally renders different text on the server and client.

Evidence:
- In [LoginComponent.tsx](/home/dmytro/Github/phd-work/nextcrm-app-update/app/[locale]/(auth)/sign-in/components/LoginComponent.tsx:36), the card title is computed as:

```ts
typeof window === "undefined" ? "Login" : "Sign in"
```

- React’s incident diff reports exactly that mismatch:
  - Server HTML: `Login`
  - Client render: `Sign in`

This is deterministic. Next.js still server-renders Client Components for the initial HTML, so `typeof window === "undefined"` is true during SSR and false during browser hydration. React then sees different text in the same node and throws the hydration mismatch.

Secondary matching issue:
- [LoginComponent.tsx](/home/dmytro/Github/phd-work/nextcrm-app-update/app/[locale]/(auth)/sign-in/components/LoginComponent.tsx:37) also branches the divider text:
  - Server: `Or continue with email`
  - Client: `Or continue with Email`

Likely introducing change:
- `git blame` points both divergent branches to commit `9be250f` from 2026-05-01: `Polish sign-in copy and labels`.
- The incident occurred on 2026-05-04, after that commit.

Confidence: high. The observed error text, route, component stack, and exact string diff all match the current source code. No code changes were made.
